[30;1m39 | [0m[35mA and B, carrying a differential voltage. In both ends of the bus is[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35ma 120 Ohm termination resistor connected between line A and B.[0m

[30;1m44 | [0m[35mWhen a logic 1 is transmitted, line A is pulled towards lower voltage and[0m
[30;1m45 | [0m[35mline B is pulled towards higher voltage.[0m
